193b5(mdo): des shi 'pho bar ston pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i tshe ldan pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten sde pa khams thams cad du mngon par byung bar spyon
193b6(mdo): dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs shing mngon par byang chub par smon pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos
193b7(mdo): kyi 'khor lo skor bar ston pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sangs rgyas kyis sems can rnams ji ltar smin cing 'dul ba'i dus ji lta ba bzhin du mkhye
193b8(mdo): bar mdzad pa ston pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sems can rnams ji ltar 'dul ba bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i dmigs pa
194a1(mdo): ba dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du brjod du med pa'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan cing / khyu mchog de bzhin gshegs pa'i thams cad mkhyen
194a2(mdo): mdzod ston pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du thams cad rnam par dag pa ston pa dang / skad cig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs
194a3(mdo): pa dang / da ltar blang ba'i sangs rgyas 'byung ba dang / dbang po dang / brtson 'grus dang / dad pa sna tshog sa kyis spyod pa'i rim pa dang / dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyis rigs mngon
194a4(mdo): bar mkhyen pa ston pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par sbubs pa'i mtshan nyid ston pa bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i
194a5(mdo): sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dus las mi 'da' ba bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgyab la
194a6(mdo): mi'ada' ba dang / dus de rnams sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas yang dag par dge ba'i rnam par smin pa'i rnam par smin pa las mi 'da' ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom
194a7(mdo): na 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas yongs su smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung ston pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas sems can gyi bsam pa
194a8(mdo): zhin cho 'phrul ston pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas sems can rnams ji ltar dad pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i phyi
194b1(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas btang snyoms la gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'da' rnams dus mkhyen nas grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal du 'jug pa dang / sang pa
194b2(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam pa dus mkhyen nas ji ltar rab du dad pa'i sems can rnam pa rab tu 'dzin pa dang / sangs rgyab bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas nyon mongs shing gdu la dga'
194b3(mdo): ba'i sems can lam brtsams pas 'dul ba dang / sangs byas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus mkhyen nas sangs rgyas kyi rnam par sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dmigs pa ston pa ste/ kye rgyal
194b4(mdo): ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dus de nas dus las mi 'da' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yul mtshungs pa med cing bsam gyis ma
194b5(mdo): pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ skyil mo krung gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par khyab pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad tshigs su bcad pa'i rtsa ba gcig yang dag par rab tu
194b6(mdo): ston pa dang / 'od zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par snang ba dang / sku gcig gis sku thams cad du ston pa dang / phyogs gcig gis gnas dmigs pas 'jig
194b7(mdo): na gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa'i rjes su 'gro ba'i sku dang / ye shes gcig gis ches thams cad bsgribs pa med par chud pa dang / dus mkhyen nas sems cig bskyed pas chos
194b8(mdo): mas cad kyi dbyings kyis ma lus par khyab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba tshad med pa'i rjes su sob
195a1(mdo): DI zhing phun sum tshogs pas grub pa dang / sangs rgyas 'gro ba nyam pa cad dang mi 'dre zhing 'das pa dang / mA 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i ngo bo nyid gcag
195a2(mdo): skye/ gnyis su med par spyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'dra ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yul mtshungs pa med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa bcu'o// kye rgyal po'i
195a3(mdo): bzhin gshegs pa rnams sangs rgyas kyi byin brlabs mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ chos thams cad la mi gnas par 'jug cing smon lam mngon par sgrub
195a4(mdo): mkhyen pa dang / lus med pa'i lus mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad gnyis su med pas mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / sems
195a5(mdo): can bdag med pa'i mthar gyur pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa la mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa
195a6(mdo): dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul thams cad ma lus pa 'jig rten gyis khams thams cad sdud pa dang 'gyur ba mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / yul thams cad la mngon par 'a/ 
195a7(mdo): da cing las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa'i dbyings su mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa yang ma
195a8(mdo): na/ rnam par byang ba yang ma yin par mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad skye ba med pa la skye zhing 'god po'i mtshan nyid rkyen dang 'du ba tshogs te byang ba mngon
195b1(mdo): bar sgrub pa mkhyen pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlab pa mngon par sgrub pa mkhyen pa bcu'o// ke rgal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom
195b2(mdo): ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa tshad med pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ dus gsum thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtags pa dang / sems can thams cad
195b3(mdo): dul ba'i cho 'phrul gsum sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos dang / gzungs dang tshigs su bcad pa'i rtsa ba rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pas
195b4(mdo): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
195b5(mdo): mas su gtogs pa dang / snying rje chen pos sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / dus thams cad du sems can thams
195b6(mdo): nga la rnam par gzigs shing rtag tu mnyam pas phan par mdzad pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas sems can thams cad 'dul ba sangs
195b7(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / ches thams cad kyi dbyings la mi chags par gnas pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / skad cig la
195b8(mdo): 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas 'byung ba thams cad sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtogs pa dang / nyi ma gcig la dus gsum gyi bskal pa
196a1(mdo): thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro zhing ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su gtag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams su
196a2(mdo): gtogs pa tshad med pa bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan dngas rnams kyi shin tu bzod par dka' ba'i chos kyi bla re bcu ste/ bcu ga nga zhi na/ bdud kyis rgol ba
196a3(mdo): com zhing gtor ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du bzod par dka' ba'i chos kyi bla re chen po dang / gzhan mur 'dug dang pa ral rgol ba thams cad char gcod pa
196a4(mdo): na du bzod par dka' ba'i chos kyi bla re chen po dang / sems can thams cad 'dul zhing tshim par mdzad pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi shin du bzod par dka' ba'i chos
196a5(mdo): rachen po dang / sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du bzod par dka' ba'i
196a6(mdo): sa kyi bla re chen po dang / chos kyi dbyings rab tu phigs shing mkhyen pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du bzod par dka' ba'i chos kyi bla/ 
196a7(mdo): khams thams cad ma lus pa'i rjes su 'gro ba'i sku gnyis su med pas sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par phye ba sangs rgyas pa com ldan 'das rnams kyi
196a8(mdo): dka' ba'i chos kyi bla re chen po dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis dbyangs kyi yan lag thams cad kyis sa so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la 'jug pa'i gnas dang / so so yang
196b1(mdo): dag par rig pa ston pa dang / sems can gti mug med cing dad pa'i sems can thos pas 'dul ba shin du bzod par dka' pa'i chos nyi bla chen po dang / phangab rgyas bcom ldan
196b2(mdo): 'ad/ rnams pa spu'i thug gcig bzhin du bsdu'i khams thams cad nam rab tu phra ba'i rdus dang mnyam pa de snyed gshegs pa gnas pa'i tshul gyis 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi hrung/ 
196b3(mdo): phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i sems can 'byin pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
196b4(mdo): shin du bzod par dka' ba'i chos kyi blar chen po'o// de bzhin gshen pa pa dkyu btsam pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gnas gcig gi rab tu tha ba'i rdul la 'jig
196b5(mdo): rten gyi khams thams cad mi rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing ston pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan rang bzhin gyis 'tsher bas chos kyi 'khor la sra zhing sems can
196b6(mdo): 'dul ba rgyun mi gcod la gtong ba med kyang gnod pa med cing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du'ang gnod pa med de/ rab tu phra ba'i rdul de rgyas par byas pa'ang med/ 'jig rten gyi khamapa
196b7(mdo): chung ngur byas pa'ang med pa chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs shing mkhyen nas gnas pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du bzod par dka' ba'i chos
196b8(mdo): pa'o// mun pa med pa'i dbyings su de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te mun pa dang bcas bsdang bar gyur nas/ sangs rgyas
197a1(mdo): bar rab rib med pa'i gnas la sems can pha rol 'dzud pa dang / de na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu'i rjes su song bA ste/ 'di ni sangs
197a2(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du bzod par dka' ba'i chos kyi bla re chen po bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi zil gyis gnod kyi
197a3(mdo): chos kyi bla re chen po bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs/ 
197a4(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tsha ba shin du bsgrubs te/ thams cad du lan ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs sngon nas
197a5(mdo): mtho bas 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi rigs thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag cing de bzhin gsheg
197a6(mdo): pa'i rigs rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam par shes pa la mi gnas shing phyi ma'i mtha' ma'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad
197a7(mdo): ba na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la gnas pa bcom zhing dus gsum la mi gnas par spyod pa ste/ 'di ni sangs
197a8(mdo): sa bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// 
197b1(mdo): pa'i ngo bo ste/ 'di ni sangs kyis bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das bsod nams zad mi
197b2(mdo): shes pas sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' mnyam pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa'i bsod nams zad mi shes pa dang ldan pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
197b3(mdo): tsha ba thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// sems can 'dul ba'i don gyi dbang gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gzugs dang kha dog mtha' med par
197b4(mdo): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na chags pa med par bzhugs te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad du khye na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// 
197b5(mdo): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'jig pa med pa bzhi brnyes te/ bag tsha ba med par gnas nas khyu mchog seng ge'i sgra sgrog ste/ stang chen po ltar rgol ba rnam par gnon cing / me mar lta
197b6(mdo): 'i kun du rtog pas chos ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad du khan ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
197b7(mdo): rjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bskal pa nas yongs su mya ngan las 'das mod kyi/ 'on kyang ming mang po rnam par rigs pas sems can
197b8(mdo): 'gas pa bzhin no// de srid du yun ring po nas yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa rnams kyang rung ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dam rnams la sbyin gnas bsnun po na yongs sub
198a1(mdo): 'gyur ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dang rnams kyi che ba thams cad du kha na ma thob med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das brjod du
198a2(mdo): med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad las ring ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams na bzhugs kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pa'i sems can gyis
198a3(mdo): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rjes su dran na sku ston par mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi che ba thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag
198a4(mdo): ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi che ba ste/ thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par dag pa bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bco
198a5(mdo): ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis sngon gyi sman lam shin du rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan
198a6(mdo): 'das kyis tshangs par spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis ma chags pa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag cing shin du rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan
198a7(mdo): 'das kyis sems can thams cad phung po las byung bar mdzad pa shin du rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing shin du rnam par dag pa
198a8(mdo): dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis g.yog 'khor shin du rnam por dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshas kyi sku shin du rnam par dag po dang / sangs rgyas
198b1(mdo): ma ldan 'das kyis gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag cing shin du rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan padas kyis myos kyi na shin du rnam par nga/ 
198b2(mdo): pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis bsgribs pa med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po shin du rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis sangs rgyas
198b3(mdo): thams cad kyi rnam par thar pa dang / rnam par gnon par mdzad pa dam pa'i mchog brnyes pa shin du rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dab rnams
198b4(mdo): shin du rnam par dag pa bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dus thams cad du 'jig rten gyi yul khams thams cad na sangs rgyam bcom ldan 'das kyis mdzad pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgya
198b5(mdo): sa su dran pa rab tu rnyed pa'i sems can rnams la dus thams cad du sangs rgyas ston pa dang / dus thams cad du sems can shes kyi sems can la chos ston pa dang / dus thams cad du
198b6(mdo): sangs rgyas la sems rab tu dang ba'i sems can pa tshad med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa dang / dus thams cad du chos mi 'gyur ba'i lam du 'das pa'i sems can la ye shes rtogs par
198b7(mdo): mdzad pa dang / dus thams cad du 'gro ba thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa rgyun mi gcod pa dang / dus thams cad du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa mi chags
198b8(mdo): par bzhud pa dang / dus thams cad du sems can thams cad la thugs rje chen po rgyun mi gcod pa dang / dus thams cad du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dape rnams rnam par sprul pa la bcus/ 
199a1(mdo): / pa dang / du ba thams cad du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas sna tshogs bu kus par bajudapa pa dang / dus thams cad du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ang/ 
199a2(mdo): rnams sangs rgyas kyi mthus chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa ste/ rje rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni dus thams cad du 'jig rten gyi yul khams thams cad na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
199a3(mdo): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes kyi rgya mtsho'i tshul ma zad
199a4(mdo): babacu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa
199a5(mdo): tshad med pa brnyes pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi yul gyi ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dra
199a6(mdo): dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi chos thams cad kyi char ba bebs pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtshom
199a7(mdo): zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang / kha dog gis ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad mkhyen pas sngon
199a8(mdo): mtha' nas smon lam spyod pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das phyi ma'i mthar 'gro ba thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa rgyun mi gcod pa'i
199b1(mdo): ci rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sems can ma lus pa'i ris thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
199b2(mdo): thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi gnon pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i/ 
199b3(mdo): sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes kyi rgya mtsho mi zad pa bcu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas pacom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi spyan bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ gang 'di ltar sangs
199b4(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams thams cad kyi pha rol du phyin cing mngon par byung ba'i spyan dang / gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos thams cad mi mkhyen pa
199b5(mdo): ma mnga' ba'i spyan dang / gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas pacom ldan 'das rnams thams cad la thugs rje che ba'i spyan dang / gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshad med pa'i
199b6(mdo): stobs bcu thams cad dang ldan pa'i spyan dang / gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba'i spyan dang / gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan
199b7(mdo): 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul bar zhugs pa'i spyan dang / gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'gro ba thams cad mdzod
199b8(mdo): nga/ gang 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzhugs pas 'dul ba'i sems can la 'dul ba'i spyan dang / gang lang

200a2(mdo): sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi mtho'i phyir sangs rgyas yongs su mya ngan las 'oda' bar ston pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi spyan bcu'o//

200b1(mdo): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag par byang chub sems dpa' rnams gyi bsam pa dang dad pa bzhin ston pa'i sgo dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad ni

200b5(mdo): sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gis kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / sangs

200b7(mdo): mas la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis sa dang / chu dang me dang / rlung gis kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / sangs
